I.  DE ADUENTU.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.3

<$$heading>

Ecce uenit rex occurramus obuiam Saluatori nostro.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.5

To dai is cumen +de holie tid +tat me clepe+d aduent.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.6

+tanked be ure louerd ihesu crist $+te $hit {TEXT:+tit} haue+d isend.
CMTRINIT-MX1,3.7

And hit laste+d +tre wuke fulle and sum del more.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.8

Et significat tria tempora.  ante legem.  subb lege.  sub gratia.
CMTRINIT-MX1,3.9

and bitocne+d +tre time.  On +te was bi-fore +te olde lage.
CMTRINIT-MX1,3.10

+te o+der was on +te holde lage.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.11

and +te +tridde was on +te newe lage.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.12

Men +te waren $wunende {TEXT:wunede} on elche of +tese +trie times wisten
gerne after ure lauerd ihesu cristes tocume alse we do+d.  +te ben on
+tesse +tre wuken; +te ben cleped aduent.  +tat is seggen on englis ure
louerd ihesu cristes tocume.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.13

Aduentus autem duo sunt manifesti.  et totidem occulti.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.14

Ure louerd ihesu cristes tocumes; ben tweien openliche.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.15

+te fireste is gon.  +to +te patriarkes and +te prophetes and o+dre men
+te waren bi +to dages after wisseden.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.16

And +tat o+der tocume be+d on domes dai.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.17

and +tat we abiden.  And alle +to; +te habben ben se+den ure louerd
ihesu crist steh to heuene.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.18

And alle +to +te ben tocumen her after abide+d his tocume.
CMTRINIT-MX1,3.19

And of +te firste tocume speke+d +te holi boc +tus que+dende.  Ecce uenit
rex et cetera.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.20

here cume+d ure king.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.21

wule we fare togenes him.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.22

and him faire understonden.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.23

and heiliche wur+die.  CMTRINIT-MX1,3.24

s.  cordis <P_5> mundicia.  oris modestia.  operis sanctimonia.
+tat is fare togenes him.  $noht lichanliche.  ac on gode +tanke.
and understonden him on ure e+dele bede.  and wur+dsupen him; on ure
edie dede.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.25

Of +de lateste to-cume spec+d +te holie boc on o+der stede +tus que+dende
.  Ecce dominus ueniet et omnes sancti eius cum eo.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.26

Ure louerd wile cume.  and alle hise halegen mid him.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.27

+tat be+d on domes dai.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.28

Tweien o+der tocumes ben bo+de iliche.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.29

Altero uisitat quando mentium tenebras illuminat.  uel caritatem cordibus
infundit.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.30

+tat o+der tocume is +tane he cume+d to men and turne+d his herte to
forleten and hatien his senne.  and to luuien god; and al his emcristen.
CMTRINIT-MX1,5.31

and +tis tocume we bidden +tane we singen.  Ueni domine uisitare nos
in pace.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.32

Cum louerd CMTRINIT-MX1,5.33

and biwind us on seihtnesse.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.34

Altero uenit rapere quemque de miseriis huius uite.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.35

+tat o+der digeliche tocume beo+d; +tane he cume+d to elch man
sunderlupes.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.36

and do+d ut of +tisse worelde.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.37

and of +tis tocume spec+d ure helende seluen on +te holie godspelle.
CMTRINIT-MX1,5.38

and muneged us alle to ben warre +tarof; CMTRINIT-MX1,5.39

and +tus que+d.  Uigilate quia nescitis diem neque horam.  +tat is be+d

Horum autem aduentum alius fuit misericordie; et ideo desiderabilis.
alius erit iusticie; et ideo formidabilis.  alius separationis;
et horridus.  alius gratie; et blandus.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.41

Of ure louerd ihesu cristes openliche tocume.  +te forme was of

and alle bileffulle men +te waren +to; and +dar biforen wissede swi+de
+dar after.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.43

and +duhte long er he come.  and alesede hem eche dea+de.
CMTRINIT-MX1,5.44

+tat o+der openliche tocume.  +tat is te cumen a domes dei; be+d of

for +tanne he wile +dere gelden elch man his hwile mid swilch mede swo

Venite benedicti patris mei et cetera.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.49

Cume+d ge ibletsede.  CMTRINIT-MX1,5.50

and underfo+d eche lif.  and blisse mid englen of heuene.  +tat is

CMTRINIT-MX1,7.55

CMTRINIT-MX1,7.56

Forwi; CMTRINIT-MX1,7.57

<$$heading>

Hora est iam nos de sompno surgere et cetera.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.66

+Te lauerd sainte powel +te is heued lor+deau of alle holie chirechen
bihield +tis wreche woreld.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.67

CMTRINIT-MX1,7.68

and him +tat sore reu.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.69

rihtlachen here liflode.  for to forleten and to beten heore synnes.
CMTRINIT-MX1,7.70

and wrot +to a writ; CMTRINIT-MX1,7.71

and +taron wi+d hem +tus spec.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.73

CMTRINIT-MX1,7.74

Hora est iam nos.  et cetera.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.75

longe we habben lein on ure fule synnes.  and swoldred +taron; alse slou
man do+d on swete slape.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.76

Ac nu hit is time.  +tat we rise $+tarof.  and clensen us of ure fule

+tus he spec+d wi+d us on stede; in his holie write.  CMTRINIT-MX1,7.78

clennesse; CMTRINIT-MX1,7.79

and +tus que+d.  Sobrie et iuste.  et pie uiuamus in hoc seculo.
CMTRINIT-MX1,7.80

Wile we leden ure lif on +tisse worelde me+deliche togenes us suluen.
+tat we +tenchen and que+den.  and do +tat ure sowle and ure lichame

CMTRINIT-MX1,9.82

Gif +tu gierne waxest on godnesse; sech after +ting +te +de be+d biheue.

help +te hauelease.  CMTRINIT-MX1,9.90

Eximi nostri omnes quibus est unus dominus.  una fides.  unum baptisma.

+De niht is for+d-gon; CMTRINIT-MX1,9.104

<heading>

IV.  {COM:Lambeth_Homily_VII} CREDO.  CMTRINIT-MX1,15.161

<$$heading>

Tria sunt hominum saluti necessaria.  scilicet fides.  baptismus uite
mundicia.  De fide aft dominus in euangelio.  Qui non crediderit
condempnabitur.  Et sapiens ait.  Sine fide inpossibile est homini
placere deo.  De baptismo autem dicit dominus in euangelio.  Nisi quis
renatus fuerit ex aqua et spiritu sancto et cetera.  De uite mundicia
dicit dominus per prophetam.  Lauamini mundi estote.  Et in psalmo.
Declina malo et fac bonum.  Et apostolus.  Immundicia nec nominetur in
uobis cupientibus igitur consequi salutem.  Insinuandum est que sit
fides catholica.  et que sit debita baptismo custodia.  et que dei
mandatorum obseruantia.  i.  uite mundicia.  Et primo que sit fidei
doctrina in simboli serie contenta.  CMTRINIT-MX1,15.163

+Dre +ting ben +tat elch man habben mot.  +te wile his cristendom leden.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.164

+tat on is rihte bileue.  CMTRINIT-MX1,15.165

+tat o+der is fulohtninge.  +te +dridde +te faire liflode.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.166

and he nis naht fulliche cristene.  +tat is ani wane of +tese +trie.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.167

Of +te bileue spec+d ure louerd ihesu crist on +te holie godspelle.
+tus que+dende.  Qui non crediderit condempnabitur.  CMTRINIT-MX1,15.168

+De man +te ne haue+d rihte bileue on him.  he be+d dempd to +tolie wowe
mid deflen on helle.  CMTRINIT-MX1,15.169

Of +te fulcninge he spec+d on o+der stede.  on +te godspelle.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.170

and sei+d.  Nisi quis renatus fuerit ex aqua et cetera.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.171

Ne mai noman cume to godes riche.  bute he be fulcned.
CMTRINIT-MX1,15.172

<P_17>

Of clene liflade spec+d ysaias +te prophete +tus que+dende.  Lauamini
mundi estote.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.174

wasse+d geu CMTRINIT-MX1,17.175

and wunie+d clene.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.176

and daui+d in +te salter boc.  A delicto meo munda me domine.
CMTRINIT-MX1,17.177

Clense me louerd of mine synnes.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.178

Et alibi.  Asperges me domine ysopo et cetera.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.179

Bispreng me mid edmodnesse louerd CMTRINIT-MX1,17.180

+tanne be ich clene.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.181

Ac for +tat elch man be+d on fulcninge of alle synnen.  and ogh to
cunnen his bileue ar he fulcninge underfo.  +tarfore ic wile segen
ow gure bileue.  and gure bede.  and tachen hit ew bi godes fultume.
CMTRINIT-MX1,17.182

+De rihte bileue setten +te twolue apostles on write; ar hie ferden in
to al middeneard to bodien cristendome.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.183

Ac elch of hem wrot his uers.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.184

and +te salme +te hie alle writen is cleped credo.  After +te formeste

and ate biginninge of cristendom; elch man leornede pater noster.
and credo; ar +tan he fulcninge understoden.  CMTRINIT-MX1,17.187
